```diff
 			<key>AllowCrash</key>
 			<true/>
 		</dict>
+		<key>MobileAssetEarlyBootTask</key>
+		<dict>
+			<key>Program</key>

+			<key>Async</key>
+			<true/>
+		</dict>

 		<dict>
 			<key>RequireSuccess</key>

```
